### [140] [A Hybrid Residue Floating Numerical Architecture with Formal Error Bounds for High Throughput FPGA Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08712)
*Mostafa Darvishi*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出混合余数浮点数值架构(HRFNA)，结合无进位余数运算与轻量级指数缩放，在FPGA上实现高达2.4倍吞吐量提升、38-55%的LUT资源节省及1.9倍能效改善，同时保持有界数值误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在FPGA平台上，浮点运算由于宽数据通路、归一化和进位传播导致成本高昂，亟需替代性数值表示方法以提升吞吐量和效率。

Method: 提出混合余数浮点数值架构(HRFNA)：形式化定义混合数值空间，证明运算与归一化的正确性，推导绝对和相对误差界限；设计完整的FPGA微架构，包含深度流水线模运算、指数管理和基于CRT的归一化引擎，实现稳态下单周期初始间隔。

Result: 在Xilinx Zynq UltraScale Plus ZCU104实现，与IEEE 754 FP32基线相比：吞吐量提升最高2.4倍，LUT减少38-55%，能效提升最高1.9倍；在点积、稠密矩阵乘法和Runge-Kutta ODE求解器上验证了稳定数值行为。

Conclusion: HRFNA在数值稳定性、动态范围和硬件效率之间占据了此前未被探索的设计空间，非常适合FPGA为中心的科学计算和CAD相关计算应用。

Abstract: Floating point arithmetic is costly on FPGA platforms due to wide datapaths, normalization, and carry propagation, motivating alternative numerical representations that improve throughput and efficiency. This paper presents the Hybrid Residue Floating Numerical Architecture (HRFNA), a fully specified numerical system that combines carry-free residue arithmetic with lightweight exponent-based scaling to achieve wide dynamic range, predictable error behavior, and efficient FPGA implementation. HRFNA is developed with a rigorous mathematical foundation: the hybrid number space is formally defined, correctness of arithmetic and normalization is proven, and explicit absolute and relative error bounds are derived, confining rounding to infrequent normalization events. A complete FPGA microarchitecture is presented, featuring deeply pipelined modular arithmetic, exponent management, and a CRT-based normalization engine that sustains an initiation interval of one cycle under steady-state operation. Application-level evaluation on dot products, dense matrix multiplication, and iterative Runge-Kutta ODE solvers demonstrates stable numerical behavior over long computation sequences. Implemented on a Xilinx Zynq UltraScale Plus ZCU104, HRFNA achieves up to 2.4 times higher throughput, 38 to 55 percent LUT reduction, and up to 1.9 times energy efficiency improvement compared to IEEE 754 FP32 baselines, while maintaining bounded numerical error. Comparative analysis shows that HRFNA occupies a previously unexplored design point between numerical stability, dynamic range, and hardware efficiency, making it well suited for FPGA-centric scientific and CAD-relevant computation.

</details>


### [141] [Unveiling the Potential of Quantization with MXFP4: Strategies for Quantization Error Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08713)
*Jatin Chhugani,Geonhwa Jeong,Bor-Yiing Su,Yunjie Pan,Hanmei Yang,Aayush Ankit,Jiecao Yu,Summer Deng,Yunqing Chen,Nadathur Satish,Changkyu Kim*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出两种软件技术（OAS和MBS），将MXFP4与NVFP4的精度差距从约10%降至1%以下，使MXFP4在保持硬件效率优势的同时达到接近NVFP4的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）对低精度格式的需求日益增长。OCP的MX标准因硬件效率优势而受关注，但其4位变体（MXFP4）在精度上落后于NVIDIA的NVFP4，限制了其应用推广。

Method: 提出两种无需硬件修改的软件技术：溢出感知缩放（OAS）通过在2的幂次方块缩放下增加有效动态范围来降低整体误差；宏块缩放（MBS）在更粗粒度上分配更高精度的缩放因子以更好地保留异常值。

Result: 在多个LLM和标准下游基准测试中，OAS和MBS将MXFP4与NVFP4的端到端精度差距从约10%平均降至1%以下，同时仅产生6.2%的平均GEMM开销。这使得MXFP4重新成为NVFP4的实用替代方案，同时保留了MX的硬件效率优势（如张量核心12%的相对面积节省）。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法成功解决了MXFP4的精度瓶颈问题，在不牺牲MX标准硬件效率优势的前提下，使其具备了与NVFP4相当的实际应用价值，为LLM的高效低精度推理提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have intensified the need for low-precision formats that enable efficient, large-scale inference. The Open Compute Project (OCP) Microscaling (MX) standard is attractive due to its favorable hardware efficiency, but its 4-bit variant (MXFP4) lags behind NVIDIA's NVFP4 in accuracy, limiting adoption. We introduce two software-only techniques, Overflow-Aware Scaling (OAS) and Macro Block Scaling (MBS), that improve MXFP4 quantization fidelity without requiring hardware changes. OAS reduces overall errors by increasing effective dynamic range under power-of-two block scaling, while MBS allocates higher-precision scaling at a coarser granularity to better preserve outliers. Across multiple LLMs and standard downstream benchmarks, OAS and MBS reduce the end-to-end accuracy gap between MXFP4 and NVFP4 from about 10% to below 1% on average, while incurring modest GEMM overhead (6.2% on average). These results re-establish MXFP4 as a practical alternative to NVFP4, enabling near-NVFP4 accuracy while retaining MX's hardware-efficiency advantages (e.g., 12% relative area savings in tensor cores).

</details>


### [142] [VeriInteresting: An Empirical Study of Model Prompt Interactions in Verilog Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08715)
*Luca Collini,Andrew Hennesee,Patrick Yubeaton,Siddharth Garg,Ramesh Karri*

TL;DR: 本文对语言模型在Verilog代码生成中的表现进行了系统性实证研究，分析了模型推理能力、专业化程度与提示工程策略之间的交互关系，揭示了不同模型类别对结构化提示和优化的响应模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型的快速发展为自动化代码生成带来了新机遇，但在模型特性与提示设计选择之间的权衡变得日益复杂。目前缺乏对Verilog代码生成领域中不同语言模型与提示策略交互作用的系统性研究，需要建立一个实证图谱来指导实践。

Method: 采用控制因子实验设计，评估了多种小型和大型语言模型（包括通用型、推理型和领域特定型）。实验涵盖基准提示、结构化输出、提示重写、思维链推理、上下文学习以及基于遗传帕累托的进化提示优化等策略，在两个Verilog基准测试集上进行系统性对比。

Result: 识别出不同模型类别对结构化提示和优化的响应模式，记录了哪些趋势能够跨模型和基准测试泛化，哪些趋势仅适用于特定的模型-提示组合。研究发现模型推理能力、专业化程度与提示工程策略之间存在复杂的交互关系。

Conclusion: 为Verilog代码生成领域的语言模型选择和提示工程实践提供了系统性指导，建立了模型特性与提示策略交互的实证框架，有助于研究人员和实践者更好地理解和利用语言模型进行硬件描述语言代码生成。

Abstract: Rapid advances in language models (LMs) have created new opportunities for automated code generation while complicating trade-offs between model characteristics and prompt design choices. In this work, we provide an empirical map of recent trends in LMs for Verilog code generation, focusing on interactions among model reasoning, specialization, and prompt engineering strategies. We evaluate a diverse set of small and large LMs, including general-purpose, reasoning, and domain-specific variants. Our experiments use a controlled factorial design spanning benchmark prompts, structured outputs, prompt rewriting, chain-of-thought reasoning, in-context learning, and evolutionary prompt optimization via Genetic-Pareto. Across two Verilog benchmarks, we identify patterns in how model classes respond to structured prompts and optimization, and we document which trends generalize across LMs and benchmarks versus those that are specific to particular model-prompt combinations.

</details>

Abstract: Compute-in-Memory (CIM) architectures have been widely studied for deep neural network (DNN) acceleration by reducing data transfer overhead between the memory and computing units. To address these challenges, this work proposes ChatNeuroSim, a large language model (LLM)-based agent framework for automated CIM accelerator deployment and optimization. ChatNeuroSim automates the entire CIM workflow, including task scheduling, request parsing and adjustment, parameter dependency checking, script generation, and simulation execution. It also integrates the proposed CIM optimizer using design space pruning, enabling rapid identification of optimal configurations for different DNN workloads. ChatNeuroSim is evaluated on extensive request-level testbenches and demonstrates correct simulation and optimization behavior, validating its effectiveness in automatic request parsing and task execution. Furthermore, the proposed design space pruning technique accelerates CIM optimization process compared to no-pruning baseline. The VerCore achieves a CoreMark score of 3261. For historical context, this is roughly equivalent to an Intel Celeron SU2300 from mid-2011 (which ran at 1.2 GHz). To our knowledge, this is the first time an autonomous agent has built a complete, working CPU from spec to GDSII. This report is organized as follows. We first review DC's design and its key components. We then describe the methodology that DC followed to build VerCore -- including RTL implementation, testbench implementation, frontend debugging, optimization to achieve timing closure, and interacting with backend tools. We review the key characteristics of the resulting VerCore. ### [145] [CktEvo: Repository-Level RTL Code Benchmark for Design Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08718)
*Zhengyuan Shi,Jingxin Wang,Tairan Cheng,Changran Xu,Weikang Qian,Qiang Xu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了CktEvo，一个面向仓库级RTL代码演化的基准测试和参考框架，通过将LLM提出的编辑与工具链反馈相结合，实现了在保持功能不变的前提下自动优化PPA（功耗、性能、面积）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在硬件设计中的应用主要集中于从自然语言提示生成或调试代码，存在歧义和幻觉问题；另一类研究从形式化输入出发，但通常只优化高层次综合或孤立模块，无法处理跨文件依赖。而实际的RTL编码是一个迭代式、仓库规模的过程，PPA源于多文件间的交互和下游工具链的共同作用，缺乏针对仓库级、跨文件依赖的LLM优化基准。

Method: 提出了CktEvo基准测试和参考框架。基准包含多个来自真实设计的高质量Verilog仓库，针对完整IP核进行测试。将任务形式化为：给定初始仓库，生成保持功能行为的同时改进PPA的编辑。框架采用闭环设计，将LLM提出的编辑与工具链反馈耦合，支持仓库规模的跨文件修改和迭代修复。

Result: 实验表明，参考框架在无需任何人工干预的情况下实现了PPA改进，验证了该方法在仓库级、功能保持、PPA驱动的RTL优化方面的有效性。

Conclusion: CktEvo为研究LLM辅助RTL优化建立了严格且可执行的基础，该优化对工程实践具有重要意义，具有仓库级、功能保持和PPA驱动的特点。

Abstract: Register-Transfer Level (RTL) coding is an iterative, repository-scale process in which Power, Performance, and Area (PPA) emerge from interactions across many files and the downstream toolchain. While large language models (LLMs) have recently been applied to hardware design, most efforts focus on generation or debugging from natural-language prompts, where ambiguity and hallucinations necessitate expert review. A separate line of work begins from formal inputs, yet typically optimizes high-level synthesis or isolated modules and remains decoupled from cross-file dependencies. In this work, we present CktEvo, a benchmark and reference framework for repo-level RTL evolution. Unlike prior benchmarks consisting of isolated snippets, our benchmark targets complete IP cores where PPA emerges from cross-file dependencies. Our benchmark packages several high-quality Verilog repositories from real-world designs. We formalize the task as: given an initial repository, produce edits that preserve functional behavior while improving PPA. We also provide a closed-loop framework that couples LLM-proposed edits with toolchain feedback to enable cross-file modifications and iterative repair at repository scale. Our experiments demonstrate that the reference framework realizes PPA improvements without any human interactions. CktEvo establishes a rigorous and executable foundation for studying LLM-assisted RTL optimization that matters for engineering practice: repository-level, function-preserving, and PPA-driven.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Automatic generation of device-level analog circuit topologies remains a fundamental challenge in analog design automation. Recent transformer-based approaches have shown promise, yet they often suffer from limited functional controllability, memorization of training data, and the generation of electrically invalid circuits. We propose AnalogToBi, a device-level analog circuit topology generation framework that addresses these limitations. AnalogToBi enables explicit functional control via a circuit type token and adopts a bipartite graph-based circuit representation that decouples positional ordering from functional semantics, encouraging structural reasoning over sequence memorization. In addition, grammar-guided decoding enforces electrical validity during generation, while apply device renaming-based data augmentation improves generalization by increasing sequence diversity without altering circuit functionality. Experimental results show that AnalogToBi achieves 97.8% validity and 92.1% novelty, resulting in 89.9% valid and novel circuits under conditional generation, without human expert involvement. We further present that generated circuits can be automatically translated into SPICE netlists, and SPICE simulations confirm that AnalogToBi discovers high-quality analog topologies that outperform prior methods. For code and supplementary materials, see https://github.com/Seungmin0825/AnalogToBi

### [148] [KernelCraft: Benchmarking for Agentic Close-to-Metal Kernel Generation on Emerging Hardware](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08721)
*Jiayi Nie,Haoran Wu,Yao Lai,Zeyu Cao,Cheng Zhang,Binglei Lou,Erwei Wang,Jianyi Cheng,Timothy M. Jones,Robert Mullins,Rika Antonova,Yiren Zhao*

Abstract: New AI accelerators with novel instruction set architectures (ISAs) often require developers to manually craft low-level kernels -- a time-consuming, laborious, and error-prone process that cannot scale across diverse hardware targets. This prevents emerging hardware platforms from reaching the market efficiently. While prior LLM-based code generation has shown promise in mature GPU ecosystems, it remains unclear whether agentic LLM systems can quickly produce valid and efficient kernels for emerging hardware with new ISAs. We present KernelCraft: the first benchmark to evaluate an LLM agent's ability to generate and optimize low-level kernels for customized accelerators via a function-calling, feedback-driven workflow. Within KernelCraft, the agent refines kernels under ISA and hardware constraints using automated feedback derived from compilation checks, simulation, and correctness validation against ground truth. In our experiments, we assess agent performance across three emerging accelerator platforms on more than 20 ML tasks, each with 5 diverse task configurations, with special evaluation of task configuration complexity. Across four leading reasoning models, top agents produce functionally valid kernels for previously unseen ISAs within a few refinement steps, with optimized kernels that match or outperform template-based compiler baselines. With that, we demonstrate the potential for reducing the cost of kernel development for accelerator designers and kernel developers.

Abstract: The inference of deep neural networks (DNNs) on resource-constrained embedded systems introduces non-trivial trade-offs among model accuracy, computational latency, and hardware limitations, particularly when real-time constraints must be satisfied. This paper presents ALADIN, an accuracy-latency-aware design-space inference analysis framework for mixed-precision quantized neural networks (QNNs) targeting scratchpad-based AI accelerators. ALADIN enables the evaluation and analysis of inference bottlenecks and design trade-offs across accuracy, latency, and resource consumption without requiring deployment on the target platform, thereby significantly reducing development time and cost.
  The framework introduces a progressive refinement process that transforms a canonical QONNX model into platform-aware representations by integrating both platform-independent implementation details and hardware-specific characteristics. ALADIN is validated using a cycle-accurate simulator of a RISC-V based platform specialized for AI workloads, demonstrating its effectiveness as a tool for quantitative inference analysis and hardware-software co-design. Experimental results highlight how architectural decisions and mixed-precision quantization strategies impact accuracy, latency, and resource usage, and show that these effects can be precisely evaluated and compared using ALADIN, while also revealing subtle optimization tensions.

### [150] [PhD Thesis Summary: Methods for Reliability Assessment and Enhancement of Deep Neural Network Hardware Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08724)
*Mahdi Taheri*

TL;DR: 本文总结了针对DNN硬件加速器的可靠性评估与增强方法的研究成果。通过系统文献综述识别研究空白，开发了新的分析性可靠性评估工具；探索了可靠性、量化和近似计算的相互关系，提出了优化计算效率与容错能力权衡的方法；并设计了实时、零开销的可靠性增强技术AdAM，在保证容错能力的同时显著降低了硬件成本。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着深度神经网络（DNN）硬件加速器的广泛应用，其可靠性问题日益凸显。然而现有的可靠性评估技术存在成本高、效率低等问题，且可靠性、量化与近似计算之间的权衡关系尚不明确，亟需开发经济高效的评估与增强方法。

Method: 1. 开展全面的系统文献综述（SLR），对现有可靠性评估技术进行分类并识别研究空白；2. 开发新的分析性可靠性评估工具；3. 探索可靠性、量化和近似计算之间的相互作用，提出优化计算效率与容错能力权衡的方法论；4. 设计实时、零开销的可靠性增强技术AdAM。

Result: 成功开发了一套经济高效的DNN硬件加速器可靠性评估工具；提出了优化计算效率与容错能力权衡的方法论；AdAM技术实现了与传统冗余方法相当的容错能力，同时显著降低了硬件成本。研究成果已应用于多个资助项目、硕士课程和工业合作中。

Conclusion: 本研究为DNN硬件加速器的可靠性评估与增强提供了新颖、经济高效的解决方案，填补了该领域的研究空白。所开发的工具和方法不仅具有重要的学术价值，还在工业界得到应用推广，推动了高效可靠的DNN硬件加速器的发展。

Abstract: This manuscript summarizes the work and showcases the impact of the doctoral thesis by introducing novel, cost-efficient methods for assessing and enhancing the reliability of DNN hardware accelerators. A comprehensive Systematic Literature Review (SLR) was conducted, categorizing existing reliability assessment techniques, identifying research gaps, and leading to the development of new analytical reliability assessment tools. Additionally, this work explores the interplay between reliability, quantization, and approximation, proposing methodologies that optimize the trade-offs between computational efficiency and fault tolerance. Furthermore, a real-time, zero-overhead reliability enhancement technique, AdAM, was developed, providing fault tolerance comparable to traditional redundancy methods while significantly reducing hardware costs. The impact of this research extends beyond academia, contributing to multiple funded projects, masters courses, industrial collaborations, and the development of new tools and methodologies for efficient and reliable DNN hardware accelerators.

### [151] [Performance Analysis of Edge and In-Sensor AI Processors: A Comparative Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08725)
*Luigi Capogrosso,Pietro Bonazzi,Michele Magno*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文综述了超低功耗边缘AI处理器（包括异构SoC、神经加速器、近传感器及传感器内计算架构），并对GAP9、STM32N6和Sony IMX500三类代表性平台进行了实证基准测试，结果表明传感器内计算（IMX500）利用率与能效-延迟积最优，MCU级（GAP9）能效最佳，神经加速器（STM32N6）延迟最低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI应用向边缘侧快速迁移，超低功耗边缘处理器架构呈现多样化发展，包括异构SoC、神经加速器及传感器内计算等范式。然而，现有文献缺乏对这些平台的统一分类与实证性能对比，难以清晰评估不同架构在始终在线和延迟敏感AI工作负载下的适用性，亟需系统综述与基准测试以指导设计选型。

Method: 1) 对商用与研究级超低功耗边缘处理器按计算范式、功耗预算与存储层次进行分类与综述；2) 选择三类代表性平台：GAP9（多核RISC-V+硬件加速器，MCU类）、STM32N6（ARM Cortex-M55+神经架构加速器，嵌入式神经加速器类）与Sony IMX500（传感器内堆叠CMOS计算，传感器内计算类）；3) 使用336M MAC的分割模型PicoSAM2，统一测试延迟、推理效率、能效及能效-延迟积。

Result: 1) 三类平台在延迟、能效、利用率上呈现明显差异：IMX500利用率最高（86.2 MAC/周期），能效-延迟积最低；GAP9在MCU功耗预算下能效最优；STM32N6原始延迟最低但能耗显著更高；2) 传感器内计算架构在利用率和能效-延迟权衡上展现明显优势，技术成熟度提升；3) 不同范式适用于不同场景：传感器内计算适合能效敏感型应用，MCU类适合功耗受限场景，神经加速器适合延迟敏感场景。

Conclusion: 传感器内计算已成为超低功耗AI处理器的重要发展方向，在利用率与能效-延迟权衡上表现突出；MCU级处理器在严格功耗预算下仍具能效优势；嵌入式神经加速器则以更高能耗换取最低延迟。未来设计需在功耗、延迟与能效间精细权衡，针对应用需求选择适配架构范式。

Abstract: This review examines the rapidly evolving landscape of ultra-low-power edge processors, covering heterogeneous Systems-on-Chips (SoCs), neural accelerators, near-sensor and in-sensor architectures, and emerging dataflow and memory-centric designs. We categorize commercially available and research-grade platforms according to their compute paradigms, power envelopes, and memory hierarchies, and analyze their suitability for always-on and latency-critical Artificial Intelligence (AI) workloads. To complement the architectural overview with empirical evidence, we benchmark a 336 million Multiply-Accumulate (MAC) segmentation model (PicoSAM2) on three representative processors: GAP9, leveraging a multi-core RISC-V architecture augmented with hardware accelerators; the STM32N6, which pairs an advanced ARM Cortex-M55 core with a dedicated neural architecture accelerator; and the Sony IMX500, representing in-sensor stacked-Complementary Metal-Oxide-Semiconductor (CMOS) compute. Collectively, these platforms span MCU-class, embedded neural accelerator, and in-sensor paradigms. The evaluation reports latency, inference efficiency, energy efficiency, and energy-delay product. The results show a clear divergence in hardware behavior, with the IMX500 achieving the highest utilization (86.2 MAC/cycle) and the lowest energy-delay product, highlighting the growing significance and technological maturity of in-sensor processing. GAP9 offers the best energy efficiency within microcontroller-class power budgets, and the STM32N6 provides the lowest raw latency at a significantly higher energy cost. Together, the review and benchmarks provide a unified view of the current design directions and practical trade-offs that are shaping the next generation of ultra-low-power and in-sensor AI processors.

</details>

Method: 基于现有分析模型，提出数据速率感知的多像素处理CNN加速器架构。通过设计空间探索来识别最优配置，在保持数据连续流动和所有硬件单元持续工作的前提下，提高硬件利用率和资源效率。

Abstract: Dataflow-based CNN accelerators on FPGAs achieve low latency and high throughput by mapping computations of each layer directly to corresponding hardware units. However, layers such as pooling and strided convolutions reduce the data at their output with respect to their input, strongly effecting the data rate of the following layers. This leads to underutilization in fully unrolled designs. While prior work introduced data-rate-aware layer-wise adaptation, determining the most efficient implementation remains challenging.
  This paper presents a data-rate-aware CNN accelerator architecture for multi-pixel processing. Building on existing analytical models, the proposed method performs design-space exploration to identify configurations that improve hardware utilization and resource efficiency while preserving continuous flow of data, keeping all hardware units busy. Experimental results show substantial reductions in arithmetic resources compared to previous designs, enabling efficient implementation of complex CNNs on a single FPGA across a wide range of data rates.

### [153] [ARKV: Adaptive and Resource-Efficient KV Cache Management under Limited Memory Budget for Long-Context Inference in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08727)
*Jianlong Lei,Shashikant Ilager*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: ARKV是一种轻量级自适应框架，通过动态分配KV缓存的精度级别，在保持约97%长上下文基准准确率的同时，将KV内存使用减少4倍，无需重新训练或架构修改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在超长上下文推理场景中部署日益增多，但KV缓存随序列长度线性增长，迅速占据GPU内存。现有内存减少技术（如驱逐和量化）依赖静态启发式方法，在严格预算下质量下降明显。

Method: ARKV在预填充阶段通过计算注意力熵、方差和峰度等统计分数，估计每层的原始量化（OQ）比率。在解码阶段，采用快速heavy-hitter评分策略，将缓存token动态分配至三种状态：原始（全精度）、量化（低精度）或驱逐。

Result: 在LLaMA3和Qwen3模型上的实验表明：长上下文任务保持约97%基线准确率，KV内存减少4倍，吞吐量损失极小；短上下文任务匹配全精度基线；在GSM8K数学推理上显著优于均匀量化。

Conclusion: ARKV为可扩展的大语言模型部署提供了实用的解决方案，实现了细粒度、数据驱动的内存控制，无需重新训练或架构修改，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in scenarios demanding ultra-long context reasoning, such as agentic workflows and deep research understanding. However, long-context inference is constrained by the KV cache, a transient memory structure that grows linearly with sequence length and batch size, quickly dominating GPU memory usage. Existing memory reduction techniques, including eviction and quantization, often rely on static heuristics and suffer from degraded quality under tight budgets. In this paper, we propose ARKV, a lightweight and adaptive framework that dynamically allocates precision levels to cached tokens based on per-layer attention dynamics and token-level importance. During a short prefill phase, ARKV estimates the original quantization (OQ) ratio of each layer by computing statistical scores such as attention entropy, variance and kurtosis. During decoding, tokens are assigned to one of three states, Original (full precision), Quantization (low precision), or Eviction, according to a fast heavy-hitter scoring strategy. Our experiments on LLaMA3 and Qwen3 models across diverse long- and short-context tasks demonstrate that ARKV preserves ~97% of baseline accuracy on long-context benchmarks while reducing KV memory usage by 4x, with minimal throughput loss. On short-context tasks, ARKV matches full-precision baselines; on GSM8K math reasoning, it significantly outperforms uniform quantization. These results highlight the practical viability of ARKV for scalable LLM deployment, offering fine-grained, data-driven memory control without retraining or architectural modifications. The source code and artifacts can be found in: https://github.com/Large-scale-Sustainable-Computing-LSC/ARKV

</details>


### [154] [Fair and Square: Replacing One Real Multiplication with a Single Square and One Complex Multiplication with Three Squares When Performing Matrix Multiplication and Convolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08732)
*Vincenzo Liguori*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出用平方运算替代乘法运算的方法：矩阵乘法和卷积中每个实数乘法可用一次平方操作渐近替代，复数乘法可用3次平方操作替代。由于平方电路的门数量约为乘法器的一半，该方法能显著减少硬件资源消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统乘法运算在硬件实现中消耗大量资源。作者观察到平方运算电路比乘法器更简单、资源消耗更少（约为一半门数量），因此探索用平方运算替代乘法运算以降低硬件成本的可行性。

Method: 提出将矩阵乘法和卷积中的实数乘法渐近替换为单一平方操作，将复数乘法替换为3次平方操作。该技术经适当调整后可应用于点积、变换等运算。设计了多种硬件架构实现，包括基于平方的脉动阵列和张量核心。

Result: 理论上证明了矩阵乘法和卷积运算中平方替代乘法的渐近可行性；在硬件实现层面，由于平方电路门数量约为同规模乘法器的一半，实现了显著的资源缩减；提出了多种硬件架构设计方案。

Conclusion: 通过平方运算替代乘法运算，可以在保持计算功能的前提下大幅降低硬件资源消耗，为高效硬件设计提供了新思路，尤其适用于矩阵乘法、卷积等核心运算场景。

Abstract: This paper shows that, for matrix multiplications and convolutions, it is possible to asymptotically replace each real multiplication with a single squaring operation. Similarly, a single complex multiplication can be replaced with 3 squaring operations. Given that an n bits squaring circuit requires about half the gate count of an nxn multiplier, this results in large resource reductions. With some caveats, the same techniques can apply to dot products, transformations and more. A varietiy of architectures implementing these ideas in hardware are described, including square based systolic arrays and tensor cores.

</details>


### [155] [Measurement-Free Ancilla Recycling via Blind Reset: A Cross-Platform Study on Superconducting and Trapped-Ion Processors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08733)
*Sangkeum Lee*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文在IQM、Rigetti和IonQ平台上评估盲重置（通过缩放序列重放实现仅含酉操作的辅助比特回收），显示可将逻辑周期延迟降低最多38倍，同时保持辅助比特清洁度≥0.86，为量子纠错中的辅助比特重用提供跨平台部署策略。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在IQM Garnet、Rigetti Ankaa-3和IonQ三个平台上，使用匹配的随机种子、序列长度和测量预算，评估盲重置（通过缩放序列重放实现仅含酉操作的回收）。测量指标包括辅助比特清洁度F_clean=P(|0>)、每周期延迟和距离为3的重复码逻辑错误代理。结合平台校准仿真，进行T1/T2敏感性映射和误差边界验证。

Conclusion: 通过跨平台实验与仿真，确定了盲重置的有效部署边界，并提供了面向后端的部署决策矩阵，为量子纠错中辅助比特重用策略的选择提供了定量依据。

Abstract: Ancilla reuse in repeated syndrome extraction couples reset quality to logical-cycle latency. We evaluate blind reset -- unitary-only recycling via scaled sequence replay -- on IQM Garnet, Rigetti Ankaa-3, and IonQ under matched seeds, sequence lengths, and shot budgets. Using ancilla cleanliness F_clean=P(|0>), per-cycle latency, and a distance-3 repetition-code logical-error proxy, platform-calibrated simulation identifies candidate regions where blind reset cuts cycle latency by up to 38x under NVQLink-class feedback overhead while maintaining F_clean >= 0.86 for L <= 6. Hardware experiments on IQM Garnet confirm blind-reset cleanliness >= 0.84 at L=8 (1024 shots, seed 42); platform-calibrated simulation for Rigetti Ankaa-3 predicts comparable performance. Architecture-dependent crossover lengths are L* ~ 12 (IQM), ~ 11 (Rigetti), ~ 1 (IonQ), and ~ 78 with GPU-linked external feedback. Two added analyses tighten deployment boundaries: a T1/T2 sensitivity map identifies coherence-ratio regimes, and error-bound validation confirms measured cleanliness remains consistent with the predicted diagnostic envelope. A deployment decision matrix translates these results into backend-specific policy selection.

### [156] [Sensitivity-Guided Framework for Pruned and Quantized Reservoir Computing Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08737)
*Atousa Jafari,Mahdi Taheri,Hassan Ghasemzadeh Mohammadi,Christian Herglotz,Marco Platzner*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对储备池计算（Reservoir Computing）的压缩框架，通过基于敏感度的剪枝机制，在量化权重中识别并移除关键性较低的权重，实现了量化、剪枝、精度与硬件效率之间的系统化权衡。实验表明，该方法在保持高精度的同时显著提升了FPGA实现的资源与能效，例如在MELBOEN数据集上，4位量化且15%剪枝率下，PDP降低50.8%，资源占用减少1.2%，精度无明显下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 储备池计算（Reservoir Computing）作为一种高效的时序建模方法，其硬件部署常面临资源与能耗约束。现有压缩技术缺乏系统化的设计空间探索，难以在量化、剪枝、精度与硬件效率之间实现精细权衡，因此需要一种能同时兼顾模型精度与硬件效率的压缩框架。

Method: 提出了一种系统化的压缩框架，核心为基于敏感度的剪枝机制：首先对储备池计算的权重进行量化，然后通过敏感性分析识别对精度影响较小的量化权重并进行剪枝，以最小化精度损失。框架支持对量化位宽、剪枝率、模型精度与硬件效率进行联合设计空间探索，并在FPGA平台上进行硬件参数评估。

Result: 在三个时序数据集（涵盖分类与回归任务）上进行了广泛实验，验证了框架的有效性。以MELBOEN数据集为例，4位量化、15%剪枝率的加速器相比未剪枝模型，资源占用减少1.2%，功耗延迟积（PDP）降低50.8%，精度无明显下降。不同配置与应用场景下均展现出资源与能效的提升，同时保持高精度。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了储备池计算在FPGA部署中的高效压缩，通过联合优化量化与剪枝，在几乎不损失精度的前提下显著降低了资源占用与能耗，为资源受限场景下的时序建模应用提供了可行的设计空间探索方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a compression framework for Reservoir Computing that enables systematic design-space exploration of trade-offs among quantization levels, pruning rates, model accuracy, and hardware efficiency. The proposed approach leverages a sensitivity-based pruning mechanism to identify and remove less critical quantized weights with minimal impact on model accuracy, thereby reducing computational overhead while preserving accuracy. We perform an extensive trade-off analysis to validate the effectiveness of the proposed framework and the impact of pruning and quantization on model performance and hardware parameters. For this evaluation, we employ three time-series datasets, including both classification and regression tasks. Experimental results across selected benchmarks demonstrate that our proposed approach maintains high accuracy while substantially improving computational and resource efficiency in FPGA-based implementations, with variations observed across different configurations and time series applications. For instance, for the MELBOEN dataset, an accelerator quantized to 4-bit at a 15\% pruning rate reduces resource utilization by 1.2\% and the Power Delay Product (PDP) by 50.8\% compared to an unpruned model, without any noticeable degradation in accuracy.

### [158] [Adaptive Multi-Objective Tiered Storage Configuration for KV Cache in LLM Service](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08739)
*Xianzhe Zheng,Zhengheng Wang,Ruiyan Ma,Rui Wang,Xiyu Wang,Rui Chen,Peng Zhang,Sicheng Pan,Zhangheng Huang,Chenxin Wu,Yi Zhang,Bo Cai,Kan Liu,Teng Ma,Yin Du,Dong Deng,Sai Wu,Guoyun Zhu,Wei Zhang,Feifei Li*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了Kareto，一个KV缓存自适应资源管理优化器，通过递减收益引导的剪枝方法高效探索配置空间并近似帕累托前沿，结合细粒度自适应调优器实现分组特定的缓存管理，在真实工作负载下相比固定配置可提升吞吐量达9.3%、降低延迟达58.3%或减少成本达20.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KV缓存的内存换计算范式对加速大语言模型推理服务至关重要，但有限的GPU高带宽内存（HBM）容量促使将KV缓存卸载到更便宜的外部存储层。这虽然扩展了容量，但引入了在变化工作负载下动态管理异构存储资源以平衡成本、吞吐量和延迟的挑战。

Method: 将问题建模为多目标优化问题，识别存储配置空间中各指标的帕累托前沿。针对目标函数非解析且存在复杂变量耦合的特点，提出Kareto优化器：1）采用递减收益引导的剪枝方法高效导航大型配置空间并近似帕累托前沿；2）引入细粒度自适应调优器，利用分层存储中的驱逐策略和KV块访问模式进行分组特定的缓存管理。

Result: 在真实工作负载追踪上的实验表明，Kareto能够适应工作负载变化，识别出更具成本效率的配置，覆盖静态策略。与1024 GB DRAM的固定配置相比，Kareto在各自优化目标下可提升吞吐量达9.3%，或降低延迟达58.3%，或减少成本达20.2%。

Conclusion: Kareto成功解决了KV缓存在异构存储资源管理中的多目标优化问题，通过高效探索配置空间和自适应调优策略，实现了成本、吞吐量和延迟之间的有效平衡，为大语言模型推理服务提供了更优的资源管理方案。

Abstract: The memory-for-computation paradigm of KV caching is essential for accelerating large language model (LLM) inference service, but limited GPU high-bandwidth memory (HBM) capacity motivates offloading the KV cache to cheaper external storage tiers. While this expands capacity, it introduces the challenge of dynamically managing heterogeneous storage resources to balance cost, throughput, and latency under varying workloads. We formulate this as a multi-objective optimization problem: identifying the Pareto frontier across these metrics within the storage configuration space. Using a high-fidelity end-to-end simulator, we observe that the objective functions are non-analytic and exhibit complex variable coupling, making the Pareto frontier difficult to approximate analytically. To obtain the frontier, we introduce Kareto, a KV-cache Adaptive REsource managemenT Optimizer. Kareto leverages a diminishing-return-guided pruning method to efficiently navigate the large configuration space and approximate the Pareto frontier. Additionally, it incorporates a fine-grained adaptive tuner that uses eviction policies in tier storage and KV block access patterns for group-specific cache management, improving cache efficiency. Experiments on real-world traces show that Kareto adapts to workload and can identify configurations of better cost efficiency, covering static strategies. Compared to the fixed setup with 1024 GB DRAM, Kareto can improve throughput by up to 9.3%, or reduce latency by up to 58.3%, or lower cost by up to 20.2% under respective optimization objectives.

However, as these technologies evolve and strive to meet the growing demands of real-life applications, the complexity of DL models continues to increase. These models require processing of massive volumes of data, demanding substantial computational power and memory bandwidth. This gives rise to the critical need for hardware accelerators that can deliver both high performance and energy efficiency. Accelerator types include ASIC based solutions, GPU accelerators, and FPGA based implementations. The limitations of ASIC and GPU accelerators have led to FPGAs becoming one of the prominent solutions, offering distinct advantages for DL workloads. FPGAs provide a flexible and reconfigurable platform, allowing model specific customization while maintaining high efficiency. This article explores various hardware level optimizations for DL. These optimizations include techniques such as loop pipelining, parallelism, quantization, and various memory hierarchy enhancements. In addition, it provides an overview of state-of-the-art FPGA-based neural network accelerators. Through the study and analysis of these accelerators, several challenges have been identified, paving the way for future optimizations and innovations in the design of FPGA-based hardware accelerators.

### [160] [The AetherFloat Family: Block-Scale-Free Quad-Radix Floating-Point Architectures for AI Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08741)
*Keita Morisaki*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出AetherFloat系列架构，通过字典序反码解包、四进制缩放和显式尾数设计，在保持精度的同时显著降低NPU硬件开销，其中AF8格式消除了LLM推理中必需的Block-Scale逻辑，实现MAC单元面积降低33.17%、功耗降低21.99%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IEEE 754浮点标准的结构要求（隐藏前导位、二进制归一化、符号-数值编码）在NPU中带来显著的面积和功耗开销；而业界转向8-bit格式（如FP8 E4M3）后，为防止LLM激活值溢出导致精度下降，强制引入了Block-Scale(AMAX)逻辑，进一步增加了硬件代价。

Method: 提出AetherFloat系列架构：采用字典序反码解包实现零周期整数比较和免分支次正规数处理；使用四进制(Base-4)缩放替代二进制归一化；采用显式尾数消除隐藏位开销；提出Vector-Shared 32-bit Galois随机舍入拓扑控制精度方差。AF8采用3-bit显式尾数，AF16作为bfloat16替代方案。

Result: 在MAC单元上实现面积减少33.17%、总功耗降低21.99%、关键路径延迟减少11.73%；AF8提供更宽动态范围，实现Block-Scale-Free属性，消除了动态缩放微架构需求；AF16通过训练后量化实现近乎无损的bfloat16替换；AF8作为QAT-first格式，在需要量化感知微调的部署场景下消除AMAX硬件。

Conclusion: AetherFloat通过从第一性原理重新设计浮点格式，在硬件效率与精度保持之间取得平衡。AF8的Block-Scale-Free特性以需要量化感知微调为代价消除了动态AMAX硬件，为LLM推理提供了一种硬件友好的低精度格式选择；AF16则提供了可直接替换bfloat16的低成本方案。

Abstract: The IEEE 754 floating-point standard is the bedrock of modern computing, but its structural requirements -- a hidden leading bit, Base-2 bit-level normalization, and Sign-Magnitude encoding -- impose significant silicon area and power overhead in massively parallel Neural Processing Units (NPUs). Furthermore, the industry's recent shift to 8-bit formats (e.g., FP8 E4M3, OCP MX formats) has introduced a new hardware penalty: the strict necessity of Block-Scaling (AMAX) logic to prevent out-of-bound Large Language Model (LLM) activations from overflowing and degrading accuracy.
  The AetherFloat Family is a parameterizable architectural replacement designed from first principles for Hardware/Software Co-Design in AI acceleration. By synthesizing Lexicographic One's Complement Unpacking, Quad-Radix (Base-4) Scaling, and an Explicit Mantissa, AetherFloat achieves zero-cycle native integer comparability, branchless subnormal handling, and a verified 33.17% area, 21.99% total power, and 11.73% critical path delay reduction across the multiply-accumulate (MAC) unit. Instantiated as AetherFloat-8 (AF8), the architecture relies on a purely explicit 3-bit mantissa. Combined with Base-4 scaling, AF8 delivers a substantially wider dynamic range, acting as a ``Block-Scale-Free'' format for inference that circumvents dynamic scaling microarchitecture. Finally, a novel Vector-Shared 32-bit Galois Stochastic Rounding topology bounds precision variance while neutralizing the vanishing gradients that plague legacy formats. While AF16 serves as a near-lossless bfloat16 replacement via post-training quantization, AF8 is designed as a QAT-first inference format: its Block-Scale-Free property eliminates dynamic AMAX hardware at the cost of requiring quantization-aware fine-tuning for deployment.

</details>


### [161] [Diagnosing FP4 inference: a layer-wise and block-wise sensitivity analysis of NVFP4 and MXFP4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08747)
*Musa Cim,Burak Topcu,Mahmut Taylan Kandemir*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了两种FP4格式（MXFP4和NVFP4）在三种规模的Qwen2.5模型上的量化敏感性，发现MLP上下投影层最敏感，门控和注意力投影层敏感性较低，且敏感层不一定集中在最后，早期层也可能高度敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FP4作为支持LLM量化的最低精度浮点格式已被前沿架构采用，但transformer内部各层的量化敏感性及其在不同FP4格式和模型规模间的泛化性尚未被充分探索。

Method: 在三种Qwen2.5模型规模（0.5B、7B、14B）上，使用受控的组件级和块级隔离方法，系统分析两种FP4格式（MXFP4和NVFP4）的量化敏感性。

Result: MLP上下投影层始终主导敏感性；门控投影层敏感性中等，注意力投影层敏感性显著较低；敏感性并非普遍集中在最后块，早期块在MXFP4下也可能高度敏感。

Conclusion: 研究提供了FP4在组件、深度和格式维度上的推理行为诊断性表征，为LLM的FP4量化实践提供了指导。

Abstract: Quantization addresses the high resource demand for large language models (LLMs) by alleviating memory pressure and bandwidth congestion and providing significantly scaled compute power with a tolerable impact on accuracy. Four-bit floating point (FP4), the lowest-precision format that preserves essential numerical properties such as exponent and sign, has begun to be adopted in cutting-edge architectures, including Blackwell and AMD CDNA, to support LLM quantization and reduce deployment costs. Although aggressive quantization can yield efficiency gains, the quantization sensitivity of within-transformer layers and whether these sensitivities generalize across existing FP4 formats and model scales remain underexplored. To elucidate quantization sensitivity, this study conducts a systematic analysis of two FP4 formats, MXFP4 and NVFP4, across three Qwen2.5 model scales (0.5B, 7B, and 14B), using controlled component-wise and block-wise isolation methodologies. We observe that MLP up- and down-projection layers consistently dominate in terms of sensitivity, while gate and attention projections are moderately and substantially less sensitive to FP4 quantization, respectively. We further find that sensitivity does not universally localize to the final blocks, but early blocks can be highly sensitive, particularly under MXFP4. Our results provide a diagnostic characterization of the inference behavior of FP4 across components, depths, and FP4 formats.

</details>


### [162] [TrainDeeploy: Hardware-Accelerated Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning of Small Transformer Models at the Extreme Edge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09511)
*Run Wang,Victor J. B. Jung,Philip Wiese,Francesco Conti,Alessio Burrello,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了TrainDeeploy框架，首次在超低功耗异构SoC上实现了支持CNN和Transformer模型的完整端侧训练流水线，通过LoRA等技术显著降低了内存需求和参数量，并在RISC-V平台上首次实现了Compact Convolutional Transformer的端到端端侧微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端侧深度神经网络微调可以实现边缘设备的长期自适应并保护数据隐私，但传统反向传播的高计算和内存需求对超低功耗、内存受限的极边缘设备构成重大挑战，尤其是架构复杂、计算规模大的注意力模型面临的挑战更为严峻。

Method: 提出TrainDeeploy框架，在异构超低功耗SoC上统一高效推理和端侧训练。该框架支持卷积神经网络和Transformer模型，并提供选择性分层微调和低秩自适应(LoRA)等多种训练策略，以实现参数高效的端侧训练。

Result: 在基于RISC-V的异构SoC上，首次实现了Compact Convolutional Transformer (CCT)的端到端端侧微调，训练速度达11张图像/秒。LoRA相比全反向传播降低动态内存使用23%，可训练参数和梯度减少15倍，内存传输量减少1.6倍。CCT模型(0.28M参数，71-126M FLOPs)达到4.6 FLOP/cycle，Deep-AE模型(0.27M参数，0.8M FLOPs)达到13.4 FLOP/cycle。

Conclusion: TrainDeeploy成功扩展了现有框架的能力，支持在极边缘平台上对CNN和Transformer模型进行参数高效的微调，为资源受限设备上的端侧训练提供了可行的解决方案，在保持数据隐私的同时实现了模型的自适应能力。

Abstract: On-device tuning of deep neural networks enables long-term adaptation at the edge while preserving data privacy. However, the high computational and memory demands of backpropagation pose significant challenges for ultra-low-power, memory-constrained extreme-edge devices. These challenges are further amplified for attention-based models due to their architectural complexity and computational scale. We present TrainDeeploy, a framework that unifies efficient inference and on-device training on heterogeneous ultra-low-power System-on-Chips (SoCs). TrainDeeploy provides the first complete on-device training pipeline for extreme-edge SoCs supporting both Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) and Transformer models, together with multiple training strategies such as selective layer-wise fine-tuning and Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA). On a RISC-V-based heterogeneous SoC, we demonstrate the first end-to-end on-device fine-tuning of a Compact Convolutional Transformer (CCT), achieving up to 11 trained images per second. We show that LoRA reduces dynamic memory usage by 23%, decreases the number of trainable parameters and gradients by 15x, and reduces memory transfer volume by 1.6x compared to full backpropagation. TrainDeeploy achieves up to 4.6 FLOP/cycle on CCT (0.28M parameters, 71-126M FLOPs) and up to 13.4 FLOP/cycle on Deep-AE (0.27M parameters, 0.8M FLOPs), while expanding the scope of prior frameworks to support both CNN and Transformer models with parameter-efficient tuning on extreme-edge platforms.

### [163] [Nemo: A Low-Write-Amplification Cache for Tiny Objects on Log-Structured Flash Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09605)
*Xufeng Yang,Tingting Tan,Jingxin Hu,Congming Gao,Mingyang Liu,Tianyang Jiang,Jian Chen,Linbo Long,Yina Lv,Jiwu Shu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出Nemo，一种针对小对象负载优化的闪存缓存设计，通过提高哈希冲突概率来增加集合填充率，从而降低应用层写放大，同时保持高内存效率和低缺失率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代存储系统普遍采用闪存SSD作为缓存层，但在小对象负载场景下，现有闪存缓存设计仍面临高写放大问题。即使使用具有低设备级写放大的先进日志结构闪存设备（如ZNS SSD和FDP SSD），应用层写放大仍然占主导地位。

Method: 提出Nemo系统，通过增强组相联缓存设计来提高哈希冲突概率，从而提升集合填充率，降低应用层写放大。具体包括：(1)引入基于布隆过滤器的索引机制，显著降低内存开销；(2)采用混合热度追踪技术，在不损失内存效率的前提下实现低缺失率。

Result: 实验结果表明，Nemo在三个关键目标上实现了良好的平衡：低写放大、高内存效率和低缺失率，同时满足了闪存缓存的各项性能要求。

Conclusion: Nemo成功解决了小对象负载下闪存缓存的高写放大问题，证明了通过合理设计可以在降低写放大的同时保持高内存效率和低缺失率，为现代存储系统的缓存层优化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Modern storage systems predominantly use flash-based SSDs as a cache layer due to their favorable performance and cost efficiency. However, in tiny-object workloads, existing flash cache designs still suffer from high write amplification. Even when deploying advanced log-structured flash devices (e.g., Zoned Namespace SSDs and Flexible Data Placement SSDs) with low device-level write amplification, application-level write amplification still dominates. This work proposes Nemo, which enhances set-associative cache design by increasing hash collision probability to improve set fill rate, thereby reducing application-level write amplification. To satisfy caching requirements, including high memory efficiency and low miss ratio, we introduce a bloom filter-based indexing mechanism that significantly reduces memory overhead, and adopt a hybrid hotness tracking to achieve low miss ratio without losing memory efficiency. Experimental results show that Nemo simultaneously achieves three key objectives for flash cache: low write amplification, high memory efficiency, and low miss ratio.

</details>

### [164] [Equitable Multi-Task Learning for AI-RANs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08717)
*Panayiotis Raptis,Fatih Aslan,George Iosifidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在线分层公平多任务学习框架（OWO-FMTL），通过内外双循环优化机制，实现了AI无线接入网中异构用户间的长期公平性，在动态场景下表现优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI无线接入网（AI-RANs）需要利用共享的边缘资源为具有时变学习任务的异构用户提供服务，现有方法难以保证用户间的公平性。如何在资源受限且动态变化的边缘环境中，确保不同用户的推理性能公平性，是该领域亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出在线分层公平多任务学习框架（OWO-FMTL），包含两个学习循环：外循环跨轮次更新共享模型，内循环在每轮内通过轻量级原始-对偶更新重新平衡用户优先级。采用广义α-公平性度量来量化公平性，实现效率与公平之间的权衡。

Result: 实验在凸优化任务和深度学习任务上进行验证，结果表明OWO-FMTL在动态场景下均优于现有的多任务学习基线方法，能够保证性能差异随时间逐渐减小，且计算开销低，适合边缘部署。

Conclusion: OWO-FMTL框架有效解决了AI-RANs中异构用户间的长期公平性问题，实现了效率与公平的灵活权衡，具备低计算开销和良好的实用性，为边缘环境下的公平多任务学习提供了可行方案。

Abstract: AI-enabled Radio Access Networks (AI-RANs) are expected to serve heterogeneous users with time-varying learning tasks over shared edge resources. Ensuring equitable inference performance across these users requires adaptive and fair learning mechanisms. This paper introduces an online-within-online fair multi-task learning (OWO-FMTL) framework that ensures long-term equity across users. The method combines two learning loops: an outer loop updating the shared model across rounds and an inner loop rebalancing user priorities within each round with a lightweight primal-dual update. Equity is quantified via generalized alpha-fairness, allowing a trade-off between efficiency and fairness. The framework guarantees diminishing performance disparity over time and operates with low computational overhead suitable for edge deployment. Experiments on convex and deep learning tasks confirm that OWO-FMTL outperforms existing multi-task learning baselines under dynamic scenarios.

### [165] [Hindsight Credit Assignment for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08754)
*Hui-Ze Tan,Xiao-Wen Yang,Hao Chen,Jie-Jing Shao,Yi Wen,Yuteng Shen,Weihong Luo,Xiku Du,Lan-Zhe Guo,Yu-Feng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出HCAPO框架，首次将后见信用分配整合至LLM智能体中，通过LLM事后评论器优化步骤级Q值估计和多尺度优势机制改进价值基线，在WebShop和ALFWorld基准上分别比GRPO提升7.7%和13.8%的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在长周期多步任务中面临稀疏奖励导致的信用分配难题。现有无价值函数方法（如GRPO）存在两个根本瓶颈：步骤级Q值估计不准确，以及中间状态的价值基线错位。

Method: 提出HCAPO框架，首次将后见信用分配（hindsight credit assignment）整合至LLM智能体。核心包括：(1)利用LLM自身作为事后评论器，通过后见推理优化步骤级Q值估计；(2)设计多尺度优势机制，在关键决策状态补充不准确的价值基线。

Result: 在WebShop、ALFWorld等三个挑战性基准上进行评估，HCAPO持续优于最先进的强化学习方法。在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct模型上，WebShop成功率提升7.7%，ALFWorld提升13.8%。实验表明HCAPO显著提升探索效率、促进简洁决策。

Conclusion: HCAPO通过后见信用分配有效解决了LLM智能体在长周期任务中的信用分配挑战，在复杂长周期任务中实现了更高的探索效率、决策质量和可扩展性，为LLM智能体的强化学习训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents often face significant credit assignment challenges in long-horizon, multi-step tasks due to sparse rewards. Existing value-free methods, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), encounter two fundamental bottlenecks: inaccurate step-level Q-value estimation and misaligned value baselines for intermediate states. To address these limitations, we introduce HCAPO, the first framework to integrate hindsight credit assignment into LLM agents. HCAPO leverages the LLM itself as a post-hoc critic to refine step-level Q-values through hindsight reasoning. Furthermore, HCAPO's multi-scale advantage mechanism effectively supplements the inaccurate value baselines at critical decision states. Evaluations across three challenging benchmarks, including WebShop and ALFWorld, demonstrate that HCAPO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art RL methods. Notably, HCAPO achieves a 7.7% improvement in success rate on WebShop and a 13.8% on ALFWorld over GRPO using the Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct model. These results indicate that HCAPO significantly enhances exploration efficiency, promotes concise decision-making, and ensures scalability in complex, long-horizon tasks.

### [166] [Generalized Reduction to the Isotropy for Flexible Equivariant Neural Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08758)
*Alejandro García-Castellanos,Gijs Bellaard,Remco Duits,Daniel Pelt,Erik J Bekkers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个将群G在积空间X×M上的不变量问题，归约为各向同性子群H在X上的不变量问题的通用框架，并成功将其应用于等变神经场，扩展了其适用范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以直接处理异质积空间（即具有不同群作用的多个空间的乘积）上的几何学习问题，需要新的理论工具来构建此类空间上的不变量函数。

Method: 证明了当群G在空间M上传递作用时，积空间X×M上的任意G-不变函数可归约为M的各向同性子群H在X上的不变量；通过建立显式的轨道等价(X×M)/G ≅ X/H，实现原理性的归约且保持表达能力。

Result: 获得了积空间不变量的显式归约定理，建立了轨道等价关系；成功将该理论应用于等变神经场，使其能处理任意群作用和齐次条件空间。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为异质积空间上的几何学习提供了原则性的解决方案，突破了现有方法的结构约束，扩展了等变神经场的适用范围。

Abstract: Many geometric learning problems require invariants on heterogeneous product spaces, i.e., products of distinct spaces carrying different group actions, where standard techniques do not directly apply. We show that, when a group $G$ acts transitively on a space $M$, any $G$-invariant function on a product space $X \times M$ can be reduced to an invariant of the isotropy subgroup $H$ of $M$ acting on $X$ alone. Our approach establishes an explicit orbit equivalence $(X \times M)/G \cong X/H$, yielding a principled reduction that preserves expressivity. We apply this characterization to Equivariant Neural Fields, extending them to arbitrary group actions and homogeneous conditioning spaces, and thereby removing the major structural constraints imposed by existing methods.

### [167] [SPREAD: Subspace Representation Distillation for Lifelong Imitation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08763)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 终身模仿学习面临灾难性遗忘挑战，现有基于L2范数的知识蒸馏方法在原始特征空间中进行匹配，对噪声和高维变异性敏感，难以保持任务表征的内在低维流形与几何结构，导致知识迁移效果不佳。

Method: 提出SPREAD框架：（1）利用奇异值分解（SVD）在低秩子空间中对齐跨任务的策略表征，保持多模态特征的底层几何结构；（2）设计置信度引导的蒸馏策略，将KL散度损失限制在top-M个最置信的动作样本上，强调可靠模式并提升优化稳定性。

Result: 在LIBERO终身模仿学习基准上的实验表明，SPREAD显著提升了知识迁移能力，有效缓解了灾难性遗忘，并取得了最先进的性能表现。

Conclusion: 通过几何结构保持的低秩子空间对齐与置信度引导的蒸馏策略，SPREAD框架为终身模仿学习提供了一种有效解决灾难性遗忘、实现稳定知识迁移的方法。

Abstract: A key challenge in lifelong imitation learning (LIL) is enabling agents to acquire new skills from expert demonstrations while retaining prior knowledge. This requires preserving the low-dimensional manifolds and geometric structures that underlie task representations across sequential learning. Existing distillation methods, which rely on L2-norm feature matching in raw feature space, are sensitive to noise and high-dimensional variability, often failing to preserve intrinsic task manifolds. To address this, we introduce SPREAD, a geometry-preserving framework that employs singular value decomposition (SVD) to align policy representations across tasks within low-rank subspaces. This alignment maintains the underlying geometry of multimodal features, facilitating stable transfer, robustness, and generalization. Additionally, we propose a confidence-guided distillation strategy that applies a Kullback-Leibler divergence loss restricted to the top-M most confident action samples, emphasizing reliable modes and improving optimization stability. Experiments on the LIBERO, lifelong imitation learning benchmark, show that SPREAD substantially improves knowledge transfer, mitigates catastrophic forgetting, and achieves state-of-the-art performance.

### [168] [Multi-level meta-reinforcement learning with skill-based curriculum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08773)
*Sichen Yang,Mauro Maggioni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多层次MDP压缩框架，通过将底层策略作为高层动作来构建层次化结构，结合课程学习实现技能迁移，从而提升序列决策问题的求解效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 序列决策问题中普遍存在多层次结构，子任务组合完成复杂目标。然而，系统性地推断和利用层次化结构一直是长期挑战。现有方法难以有效捕捉和利用这种自然层次结构，导致求解复杂MDP时效率低下。

Method: 提出一种高效的多层次MDP压缩过程：(1)将某一层次的参数化策略族视为更高层次压缩MDP中的单一动作，保留原始MDP的语义和结构；(2)高层MDP是独立的、随机性更小的MDP，可用现有算法求解；(3)空间或时间尺度在高层被粗化，便于寻找长期最优策略；(4)策略分解为嵌入（问题特定）和技能（含高阶函数），促进跨问题和跨层次的技能迁移；(5)整个过程嵌入课程学习框架，教师智能体逐步增加任务难度并促进跨MDP和跨层次的迁移。

Result: 多层次表示解耦了子任务，大幅减少不必要的随机性和策略搜索空间，求解MDP时需要更少的迭代和计算。该方法保证了抽象、可迁移性和课程学习的一致性。在包括MazeBase+（MazeBase的复杂变体）等多个示例中验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 在温和假设下可保证框架的一致性和优势。该方法成功实现了抽象、迁移学习和课程学习，为层次化强化学习提供了新的理论框架和实践方法，能够更高效地解决复杂序列决策问题。

Abstract: We consider problems in sequential decision making with natural multi-level structure, where sub-tasks are assembled together to accomplish complex goals. Systematically inferring and leveraging hierarchical structure has remained a longstanding challenge; we describe an efficient multi-level procedure for repeatedly compressing Markov decision processes (MDPs), wherein a parametric family of policies at one level is treated as single actions in the compressed MDPs at higher levels, while preserving the semantic meanings and structure of the original MDP, and mimicking the natural logic to address a complex MDP. Higher-level MDPs are themselves independent MDPs with less stochasticity, and may be solved using existing algorithms. As a byproduct, spatial or temporal scales may be coarsened at higher levels, making it more efficient to find long-term optimal policies. The multi-level representation delivered by this procedure decouples sub-tasks from each other and usually greatly reduces unnecessary stochasticity and the policy search space, leading to fewer iterations and computations when solving the MDPs. A second fundamental aspect of this work is that these multi-level decompositions plus the factorization of policies into embeddings (problem-specific) and skills (including higher-order functions) yield new transfer opportunities of skills across different problems and different levels. This whole process is framed within curriculum learning, wherein a teacher organizes the student agent's learning process in a way that gradually increases the difficulty of tasks and and promotes transfer across MDPs and levels within and across curricula. The consistency of this framework and its benefits can be guaranteed under mild assumptions. We demonstrate abstraction, transferability, and curriculum learning in examples, including MazeBase+, a more complex variant of the MazeBase example.

### [169] [The Temporal Markov Transition Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08803)
*Michael Leznik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了时间马尔可夫转移场（TMTF），通过将时间序列分段并估计局部转移矩阵，解决了传统MTF在非平稳过程中丢失时间信息的问题，生成能够保留时序动态变化信息的二维图像表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统马尔可夫转移场（MTF）使用全局转移矩阵编码时间序列，在平稳过程下表现良好，但当过程存在阶段性变化（regime changes）时，全局矩阵会平均化不同阶段的动态特性，导致生成的图像丢失了各动态阶段的时序信息，无法反映"何时"发生了动态变化。

Method: 提出时间马尔可夫转移场（TMTF）方法：将时间序列划分为K个连续时间块（temporal chunks），为每个块估计独立的局部转移矩阵，并构建T×T的二维图像，使得每一行反映其所属时间块的局部动态而非全局平均。图像呈现K个水平带状区域，每个带状区域编码一个时间段的转移动态。

Result: TMTF生成的图像具有K个不同纹理的水平带状结构，每个带状区域编码对应时间段的转移动态特性。方法保持了幅度无关性和保序性，适合作为卷积神经网络的输入通道用于时间序列表征任务。论文分析了时间分块引入的偏差-方差权衡，并给出了局部转移矩阵在过程属性（如持续性、均值回归、趋势行为）方面的几何解释。

Conclusion: TMTF成功扩展了传统MTF方法，能够有效捕捉非平稳时间序列中的时序动态变化信息，为时间序列分类和表征任务提供了更合适的图像表示方法，特别适用于具有阶段性变化特征的时间序列分析。

Abstract: The Markov Transition Field (MTF), introduced by Wang and Oates (2015), encodes a time series as a two-dimensional image by mapping each pair of time steps to the transition probability between their quantile states, estimated from a single global transition matrix. This construction is efficient when the transition dynamics are stationary, but produces a misleading representation when the process changes regime over time: the global matrix averages across regimes and the resulting image loses all information about \emph{when} each dynamical regime was active. In this paper we introduce the \emph{Temporal Markov Transition Field} (TMTF), an extension that partitions the series into $K$ contiguous temporal chunks, estimates a separate local transition matrix for each chunk, and assembles the image so that each row reflects the dynamics local to its chunk rather than the global average. The resulting $T \times T$ image has $K$ horizontal bands of distinct texture, each encoding the transition dynamics of one temporal segment. We develop the formal definition, establish the key structural properties of the representation, work through a complete numerical example that makes the distinction from the global MTF concrete, analyse the bias--variance trade-off introduced by temporal chunking, and discuss the geometric interpretation of the local transition matrices in terms of process properties such as persistence, mean reversion, and trending behaviour. The TMTF is amplitude-agnostic and order-preserving, making it suitable as an input channel for convolutional neural networks applied to time series characterisation tasks.

</details>

Method: 开发了SoftJAX和SoftTorch两个功能完整的开源库，提供软函数作为JAX和PyTorch硬算子的即插即用替代品。库包含：(i) 逐元素算子（如clip、abs），(ii) 通过模糊逻辑处理布尔值和索引的工具方法，(iii) 基于最优传输或置换多面体投影的轴操作算子（如sort、rank），(iv) 完整支持直通梯度估计。

Result: 成功实现了多样化的软松弛算子库，支持可微分编程中的常见操作，并通过基准测试和实际案例研究验证了库的可用性和有效性。代码已在GitHub开源。

Conclusion: SoftJAX和SoftTorch使软松弛工具箱易于在可微分编程中使用，为科学计算中的梯度优化提供了统一的解决方案。

Abstract: Automatic differentiation (AD) frameworks such as JAX and PyTorch have enabled gradient-based optimization for a wide range of scientific fields. Yet, many "hard" primitives in these libraries such as thresholding, Boolean logic, discrete indexing, and sorting operations yield zero or undefined gradients that are not useful for optimization. While numerous "soft" relaxations have been proposed that provide informative gradients, the respective implementations are fragmented across projects, making them difficult to combine and compare. This work introduces SoftJAX and SoftTorch, open-source, feature-complete libraries for soft differentiable programming. These libraries provide a variety of soft functions as drop-in replacements for their hard JAX and PyTorch counterparts. This includes (i) elementwise operators such as clip or abs, (ii) utility methods for manipulating Booleans and indices via fuzzy logic, (iii) axiswise operators such as sort or rank -- based on optimal transport or permutahedron projections, and (iv) offer full support for straight-through gradient estimation. Overall, SoftJAX and SoftTorch make the toolbox of soft relaxations easily accessible to differentiable programming, as demonstrated through benchmarking and a practical case study. Code is available at github.com/a-paulus/softjax and github.com/a-paulus/softtorch.

### [172] [Strategically Robust Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Linear Function Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09208)
*Jake Gonzales,Max Horwitz,Eric Mazumdar,Lillian J. Ratliff*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对一般和马尔可夫博弈中纳什均衡计算的困难性和脆弱性，提出了风险敏感量子响应均衡（RQRE）及其求解算法RQRE-OVI，通过有限样本遗憾分析证明了算法的收敛性，并揭示了性能与鲁棒性之间的帕累托权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体强化学习中，一般和马尔可夫博弈的纳什均衡计算面临核心挑战：计算上不可行、均衡多重性导致的脆弱性，以及对近似误差的敏感性。这些局限性亟需一种更鲁棒、更易计算的均衡解概念。

Abstract: Provably efficient and robust equilibrium computation in general-sum Markov games remains a core challenge in multi-agent reinforcement learning. Nash equilibrium is computationally intractable in general and brittle due to equilibrium multiplicity and sensitivity to approximation error. We study Risk-Sensitive Quantal Response Equilibrium (RQRE), which yields a unique, smooth solution under bounded rationality and risk sensitivity. We propose \texttt{RQRE-OVI}, an optimistic value iteration algorithm for computing RQRE with linear function approximation in large or continuous state spaces. Through finite-sample regret analysis, we establish convergence and explicitly characterize how sample complexity scales with rationality and risk-sensitivity parameters. The regret bounds reveal a quantitative tradeoff: increasing rationality tightens regret, while risk sensitivity induces regularization that enhances stability and robustness. This exposes a Pareto frontier between expected performance and robustness, with Nash recovered in the limit of perfect rationality and risk neutrality. We further show that the RQRE policy map is Lipschitz continuous in estimated payoffs, unlike Nash, and RQRE admits a distributionally robust optimization interpretation. Empirically, we demonstrate that \texttt{RQRE-OVI} achieves competitive performance under self-play while producing substantially more robust behavior under cross-play compared to Nash-based approaches. These results suggest \texttt{RQRE-OVI} offers a principled, scalable, and tunable path for equilibrium learning with improved robustness and generalization.

Conclusion: 消息传递GNN在适当设计下可作为离散扩散模型的高效骨干网络，在保持生成质量的同时显著提升计算效率，为图生成领域提供了比Transformer更轻量的替代方案。

Abstract: Discrete graph generation has emerged as a powerful paradigm for modeling graph data, often relying on highly expressive neural backbones such as transformers or higher-order architectures. We revisit this design choice by introducing GenGNN, a modular message-passing framework for graph generation. Diffusion models with GenGNN achieve more than 90% validity on Tree and Planar datasets, within margins of graph transformers, at 2-5x faster inference speed. For molecule generation, DiGress with a GenGNN backbone achieves 99.49% Validity. A systematic ablation study shows the benefit provided by each GenGNN component, indicating the need for residual connections to mitigate oversmoothing on complicated graph-structure. Through scaling analyses, we apply a principled metric-space view to investigate learned diffusion representations and uncover whether GNNs can be expressive neural backbones for discrete diffusion.

In this paper, we study this question, focusing on a broad family of core synthetic tasks. For this family of tasks, we prove the existence of fundamental limitations for non-hybrid models. Specifically, any Transformer or state-space model that solves the underlying task requires either a large number of parameters or a large working memory. ### [176] [A New Modeling to Feature Selection Based on the Fuzzy Rough Set Theory in Normal and Optimistic States on Hybrid Information Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08900)
*Mohammad Hossein Safarpour,Seyed Mohammad Alavi,Mohammad Izadikhah,Hossein Dibachi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在UCI标准数据集上进行了测试，并与其他算法进行了对比。实验结果表明，FSbuHD模型在特征选择方面具有更高的效率和有效性，相比以往的方法和算法表现优异。

Abstract: Considering the high volume, wide variety, and rapid speed of data generation, investigating feature selection methods for big data presents various applications and advantages. By removing irrelevant and redundant features, feature selection reduces data dimensions, thereby facilitating optimal decision-making within decision systems. One of the key tools for feature selection in hybrid information systems is fuzzy rough set theory. However, this theory faces two significant challenges: First, obtaining fuzzy equivalence relations through intersection operations in high-dimensional spaces can be both time-consuming and memory-intensive. Additionally, this method may produce noisy data, complicating the feature selection process. The purpose and innovation of this paper are to address these issues. We proposed a new feature selection model that calculates the combined distance between objects and subsequently used this information to derive the fuzzy equivalence relation. Rather than directly solving the feature selection problem, this approach reformulates it into an optimization problem that can be tackled using appropriate meta-heuristic algorithms. We have named this new approach FSbuHD. The FSbuHD model operates in two modes - normal and optimistic - based on the selection of one of the two introduced fuzzy equivalence relations. The model is then tested on standard datasets from the UCI repository and compared with other algorithms. The results of this research demonstrate that FSbuHD is one of the most efficient and effective methods for feature selection when compared to previous methods and algorithms.

### [177] [Cross-Domain Uncertainty Quantification for Selective Prediction: A Comprehensive Bound Ablation with Transfer-Informed Betting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08907)
*Abhinaba Basu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了选择性预测风险控制的九种有限样本边界族，提出迁移引导博弈（TIB）方法，通过源域风险信息热启动WSR财富过程，在小样本场景下显著收紧边界。实验显示，在MASSIVE数据集上LTT相比Hoeffding提升27%覆盖率，在NyayaBench小样本场景下TIB相比基线提升5.4倍覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 选择性预测需要有限样本边界提供风险保证，但现有方法在小样本场景下边界过松。集中不等式（如Hoeffding）在样本稀缺时过于保守，且域适应场景缺乏有效的边界传递机制。需要系统评估不同边界族并开发能利用源域信息的新方法。

Method: 系统对比九种有限样本边界族，结合集中不等式（Hoeffding、经验Bernstein、Clopper-Pearson、Wasserstein DRO、CVaR）与多重检验校正（union bound、LTT固定序列）及博弈序列（WSR）。提出迁移引导博弈（TIB），用源域风险轮廓热启动WSR财富过程，证明其在所有源-目标域散度下保持有效supermartingale性质，且在域匹配时主导标准WSR。

Result: 在四个基准（MASSIVE、NyayaBench、CLINC-150、Banking77）上评估18种(α,δ)配置。MASSIVE上α=0.10时LTT消除ln(K)惩罚，达94.0%保证覆盖率vs Hoeffding的73.8%（相对提升27%）。NyayaBench小样本场景下TIB在α=0.10时达18.5%覆盖率，比LTT+Hoeffding提升5.4倍。与split-conformal对比显示选择性预测提供单一预测风险保证。应用于代理缓存系统，形式化渐进信任模型。

Conclusion: 迁移引导博弈（TIB）成功利用源域信息收紧小样本边界，LTT消除union bound惩罚，二者结合在选择性预测风险控制中实现显著改进。博弈序列、LTT单调检验与跨域迁移的三重组合为文献首创。方法已成功应用于代理缓存系统的渐进信任建模。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive ablation of nine finite-sample bound families for selective prediction with risk control, combining concentration inequalities (Hoeffding, Empirical Bernstein, Clopper-Pearson, Wasserstein DRO, CVaR) with multiple-testing corrections (union bound, Learn Then Test fixed-sequence) and betting-based confidence sequences (WSR). Our main theoretical contribution is Transfer-Informed Betting (TIB), which warm-starts the WSR wealth process using a source domain's risk profile, achieving tighter bounds in data-scarce settings with a formal dominance guarantee. We prove that the TIB wealth process remains a valid supermartingale under all source-target divergences, that TIB dominates standard WSR when domains match, and that no data-independent warm-start can achieve better convergence. The combination of betting-based confidence sequences, LTT monotone testing, and cross-domain transfer is, to our knowledge, a three-way novelty not present in the literature. We evaluate all nine bound families on four benchmarks-MASSIVE (n=1,102), NyayaBench (n=280), CLINC-150 (n=22.5K), and Banking77 (n=13K)-across 18 (alpha, delta) configurations. On MASSIVE at alpha=0.10, LTT eliminates the ln(K) union-bound penalty, achieving 94.0% guaranteed coverage versus 73.8% for Hoeffding-a 27% relative improvement. On NyayaBench, where the small calibration set makes Hoeffding-family bounds infeasible below alpha=0.20, Transfer-Informed Betting achieves 18.5% coverage at alpha=0.10, a 5.4x improvement over LTT + Hoeffding. We additionally compare with split-conformal prediction, showing that conformal methods produce prediction sets (avg. 1.67 classes) whereas selective prediction provides single-prediction risk guarantees. We apply these methods to agentic caching systems, formalizing a progressive trust model where the guarantee determines when cached responses can be served autonomously.

### [178] [Quantifying Memorization and Privacy Risks in Genomic Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08913)
*Alexander Nemecek,Wenbiao Li,Xiaoqian Jiang,Jaideep Vaidya,Erman Ayday*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基因组语言模型越来越多地在敏感基因组数据上进行训练或微调，存在记忆特定训练序列的风险，引发隐私泄露、数据泄露和监管合规等严重问题。然而，目前缺乏针对基因组领域的系统性记忆化风险评估，而基因组数据具有独特的属性，如固定的核苷酸字母表、强生物结构和个体可识别性。

Method: 提出了一个综合的多向量隐私评估框架，整合了三种互补的风险评估方法：基于困惑度的检测、金丝雀序列提取和成员推断。这些方法被组合成一个统一的评估管道，生成最坏情况下的记忆化风险评分。为了实现可控评估，研究者在合成和真实基因组数据集中以不同重复率植入金丝雀序列，从而精确量化重复和训练动态如何影响记忆化。框架在多种GLM架构上进行了评估。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了GLMs记忆化风险的系统性评估方法，证明了多向量隐私审计框架对于全面理解和量化基因组语言模型隐私风险的重要性，为基因组AI系统的隐私保护实践提供了重要的方法论支持和实证依据。

Abstract: Genomic language models (GLMs) have emerged as powerful tools for learning representations of DNA sequences, enabling advances in variant prediction, regulatory element identification, and cross-task transfer learning. However, as these models are increasingly trained or fine-tuned on sensitive genomic cohorts, they risk memorizing specific sequences from their training data, raising serious concerns around privacy, data leakage, and regulatory compliance. Despite growing awareness of memorization risks in general-purpose language models, little systematic evaluation exists for these risks in the genomic domain, where data exhibit unique properties such as a fixed nucleotide alphabet, strong biological structure, and individual identifiability. We present a comprehensive, multi-vector privacy evaluation framework designed to quantify memorization risks in GLMs. Our approach integrates three complementary risk assessment methodologies: perplexity-based detection, canary sequence extraction, and membership inference. These are combined into a unified evaluation pipeline that produces a worst-case memorization risk score. To enable controlled evaluation, we plant canary sequences at varying repetition rates into both synthetic and real genomic datasets, allowing precise quantification of how repetition and training dynamics influence memorization. We evaluate our framework across multiple GLM architectures, examining the relationship between sequence repetition, model capacity, and memorization risk. Our results establish that GLMs exhibit measurable memorization and that the degree of memorization varies across architectures and training regimes. These findings reveal that no single attack vector captures the full scope of memorization risk, underscoring the need for multi-vector privacy auditing as a standard practice for genomic AI systems.

### [179] [Uncovering a Winning Lottery Ticket with Continuously Relaxed Bernoulli Gates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08914)
*Itamar Tsayag,Ofir Lindenbaum*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个全可微分的强彩票假设(SLT)发现方法，通过连续松弛的伯努利门机制，在冻结网络权重的情况下仅训练门控参数，实现了高达90%的稀疏度且精度损失极小，稀疏度约为现有方法(edge-popup)的两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过参数化神经网络在资源受限场景下部署成本高昂。现有的强彩票假设方法（如edge-popup）依赖不可微的基于分数的选择机制，限制了优化效率和可扩展性。因此，需要一种更高效、可微分的方法来发现稀疏子网络。

Method: 提出使用连续松弛的伯努利门(continuously relaxed Bernoulli gates)来发现强彩票子网络。该方法保持所有网络权重冻结在初始化值，仅训练门控参数，实现了端到端的全可微分优化。通过连续松弛技术，可以直接对ℓ₀正则化目标进行基于梯度的优化，无需不可微的梯度估计器或迭代剪枝循环。

Result: 在全连接网络、CNN(ResNet, Wide-ResNet)和视觉Transformer(ViT, Swin-T)上的实验表明，该方法在精度损失极小的情况下实现了高达90%的稀疏度。在相近精度下，稀疏度约为edge-popup方法的两倍，证明了该方法的优越性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了首个无需直通估计器近似的全可微分SLT发现框架，为预训练网络稀疏化提供了一个可扩展的解决方案，显著提升了稀疏度和优化效率。

Abstract: Over-parameterized neural networks incur prohibitive memory and computational costs for resource-constrained deployment. The Strong Lottery Ticket (SLT) hypothesis suggests that randomly initialized networks contain sparse subnetworks achieving competitive accuracy without weight training. Existing SLT methods, notably edge-popup, rely on non-differentiable score-based selection, limiting optimization efficiency and scalability. We propose using continuously relaxed Bernoulli gates to discover SLTs through fully differentiable, end-to-end optimization - training only gating parameters while keeping all network weights frozen at their initialized values. Continuous relaxation enables direct gradient-based optimization of an $\ell_0$-regularization objective, eliminating the need for non-differentiable gradient estimators or iterative pruning cycles. To our knowledge, this is the first fully differentiable approach for SLT discovery that avoids straight-through estimator approximations. Experiments across fully connected networks, CNNs (ResNet, Wide-ResNet), and Vision Transformers (ViT, Swin-T) demonstrate up to 90% sparsity with minimal accuracy loss - nearly double the sparsity achieved by edge-popup at comparable accuracy - establishing a scalable framework for pre-training network sparsification.

### [180] [The $qs$ Inequality: Quantifying the Double Penalty of Mixture-of-Experts at Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08960)
*Vignesh Adhinarayanan,Nuwan Jayasena*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MoE模型在推理时面临"复用碎片化"问题，导致吞吐量显著下降。本文提出qs不等式预测MoE相对于等效稠密模型的劣势，发现DeepSeek-V3在128k上下文时吞吐量比稠密模型低4.5倍，建议将MoE视为训练优化手段，推理时蒸馏为稠密模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE模型在训练时具有FLOPs优势，但推理效率常被忽视。作者发现MoE在解码时存在双重惩罚：专家路由导致微批次碎片化和权重复用减少；大量常驻专家池占用HBM，减少KV缓存空间。这种"复用碎片化"现象使FFN进入带宽受限状态，尤其在长上下文场景下问题严重。

Method: 提出qs不等式作为预测准则，用于判断MoE是否相对于质量等效的稠密模型存在结构性劣势。该准则统一了稀疏度s（每token激活参数比例）和质量等效因子q（稠密模型达到MoE性能所需的规模倍数）。在DeepSeek-V3、Qwen3-235B、Grok-1和Switch-C等前沿模型上进行验证。

Result: 复用碎片化是普遍的架构现象。在128k上下文场景下，DeepSeek-V3相比质量等效的稠密基准吞吐量低4.5倍。大型架构如Switch-C在某些集群规模下变得不可行，而等效稠密模型仍可运行。

Conclusion: 训练时FLOP效率不能完整反映长上下文推理性能。MoE更适合被视为训练时优化手段，蒸馏为稠密模型可能是推理高效部署的有效路径。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models deliver high quality at low training FLOPs, but this efficiency often vanishes at inference. We identify a double penalty that structurally disadvantages MoE architectures during decoding: first, expert routing fragments microbatches and reduces weight reuse; second, massive resident expert pools reduce high-bandwidth memory (HBM) headroom for the KV cache. This phenomenon, formalized as reuse fragmentation, pushes feed-forward networks (FFNs) into a bandwidth-bound regime, especially at long context lengths.
  We introduce the $qs$ inequality, a predictive criterion that identifies when MoE is structurally disadvantaged relative to a quality-matched dense model. This criterion unifies sparsity ($s$), the fraction of parameters activated per token, and the quality-equivalence factor ($q$), the size multiplier required for a dense model to match MoE performance. Our evaluation across frontier models including DeepSeek-V3, Qwen3-235B, Grok-1, and Switch-C demonstrates that this fragmentation is a general architectural phenomenon. For DeepSeek-V3 at 128k context, this results in a 4.5x throughput advantage for a quality-matched dense baseline. Crucially, massive architectures like Switch-C can become infeasible on cluster sizes where a quality-matched dense model remains viable.
  Our results suggest that training-time FLOP efficiency is an incomplete proxy for inference-time performance in long-context serving. They also indicate that MoE may be best viewed as a training-time optimization, with distillation into dense models as a possible path toward inference-efficient deployment.

</details>


### [181] [Semantic Level of Detail: Multi-Scale Knowledge Representation via Heat Kernel Diffusion on Hyperbolic Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08965)
*Edward Izgorodin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了语义细节层次（SLoD）框架，通过在庞加莱球上的热核扩散定义连续缩放算子，实现了知识图谱中抽象层次边界的自动发现与导航。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI记忆系统日益采用图结构组织知识（知识图谱、实体关系、社区层次），但缺乏连续分辨率控制的原理性机制：抽象层次之间的定性边界在哪里？智能体应如何导航这些层次？现有方法需要手动设定分辨率参数，缺乏理论指导。

Method: 提出语义细节层次（SLoD）框架：(1)在庞加莱球$\mathbb{B}^d$上通过热核扩散定义连续缩放算子；(2)粗尺度（$\sigma\to\infty$）时扩散将嵌入聚合为高层摘要，细尺度（$\sigma\to 0$）时保留局部语义细节；(3)证明在Sarkar嵌入下树结构层次具有层次一致性和有界逼近误差$O(\sigma)$及$(1+\varepsilon)$失真；(4)利用图拉普拉斯算子的谱间隙自动检测表示发生定性转变的尺度边界，无需手动分辨率参数。

Result: 在合成层次结构（HSBM）上，边界扫描器恢复植入层次的调整兰德指数（ARI）高达1.00，在信息论Kesten-Stigum阈值附近检测性能优雅降级；在完整WordNet名词层次（82K同义词集）上，检测到的边界与真实分类学深度对齐（$\tau=0.79$），证明该方法能在无监督下发现真实知识图谱中有意义的抽象层次。

Conclusion: SLoD框架为AI记忆系统提供了首个原理性的连续分辨率控制机制，通过谱间隙自动发现抽象层次边界，在理论和实验上均验证了方法的有效性，为知识图谱中的层次导航提供了新的理论基础和实用工具。

Abstract: AI memory systems increasingly organize knowledge into graph structures -- knowledge graphs, entity relations, community hierarchies -- yet lack a principled mechanism for continuous resolution control: where do the qualitative boundaries between abstraction levels lie, and how should an agent navigate them? We introduce Semantic Level of Detail (SLoD), a framework that answers both questions by defining a continuous zoom operator via heat kernel diffusion on the Poincaré ball $\mathbb{B}^d$. At coarse scales ($σ\to \infty$), diffusion aggregates embeddings into high-level summaries; at fine scales ($σ\to 0$), local semantic detail is preserved. We prove hierarchical coherence with bounded approximation error $O(σ)$ and $(1+\varepsilon)$ distortion for tree-structured hierarchies under Sarkar embedding. Crucially, we show that spectral gaps in the graph Laplacian induce emergent scale boundaries -- scales where the representation undergoes qualitative transitions -- which can be detected automatically without manual resolution parameters. On synthetic hierarchies (HSBM), our boundary scanner recovers planted levels with ARI up to 1.00, with detection degrading gracefully near the information-theoretic Kesten-Stigum threshold. On the full WordNet noun hierarchy (82K synsets), detected boundaries align with true taxonomic depth ($τ= 0.79$), demonstrating that the method discovers meaningful abstraction levels in real-world knowledge graphs without supervision.

### [182] [MAcPNN: Mutual Assisted Learning on Data Streams with Temporal Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08972)
*Federico Giannini,Emanuele Della Valle*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网数据分析中，传统机器学习范式在处理数据流时面临持续学习、概念漂移、时序依赖和遗忘等挑战。现有联邦学习方法要求设备在每轮训练时都进行通信，导致通信开销大。本文旨在通过边缘设备间的按需知识共享，在减少通信的同时提升模型性能。

Method: 提出互助学习范式，每个边缘设备配备连续渐进神经网络（cPNN）以处理动态数据流。当设备因概念漂移导致性能下降时，主动向其他设备请求协助并评估其知识的有用性。该框架无需中央协调器，采用单数据点预测和量化技术以减少内存占用。

Result: 实验结果表明，MAcPNN在合成和真实数据流上均能有效提升性能。与传统联邦学习相比，该方法大幅减少了设备间的连接次数，同时保持了良好的学习效果。

Conclusion: MAcPNN为物联网边缘设备提供了一种高效的去中心化持续学习解决方案，通过按需互助机制有效应对概念漂移，在降低通信成本的同时提升了模型性能。

Abstract: Internet of Things (IoT) Analytics often involves applying machine learning (ML) models on data streams. In such scenarios, traditional ML paradigms face obstacles related to continuous learning while dealing with concept drifts, temporal dependence, and avoiding forgetting. Moreover, in IoT, different edge devices build up a network. When learning models on those devices, connecting them could be useful in improving performance and reusing others' knowledge. This work proposes Mutual Assisted Learning, a learning paradigm grounded on Vygotsky's popular Sociocultural Theory of Cognitive Development. Each device is autonomous and does not need a central orchestrator. Whenever it degrades its performance due to a concept drift, it asks for assistance from others and decides whether their knowledge is useful for solving the new problem. This way, the number of connections is drastically reduced compared to the classical Federated Learning approaches, where the devices communicate at each training round. Every device is equipped with a Continuous Progressive Neural Network (cPNN) to handle the dynamic nature of data streams. We call this implementation Mutual Assisted cPNN (MAcPNN). To implement it, we allow cPNNs for single data point predictions and apply quantization to reduce the memory footprint. Experimental results prove the effectiveness of MAcPNN in boosting performance on synthetic and real data streams.

Method: 提出归一化流匹配（NFM）方法：首先利用预训练的自回归（AR）NF模型获得准确定性耦合，然后将该耦合蒸馏到学生流模型中进行训练。该方法不直接计算自适应耦合，而是从预训练模型中提取耦合信息。

Abstract: Flow models have rapidly become the go-to method for training and deploying large-scale generators, owing their success to inference-time flexibility via adjustable integration steps. A crucial ingredient in flow training is the choice of coupling measure for sampling noise/data pairs that define the flow matching (FM) regression loss. While FM training defaults usually to independent coupling, recent works show that adaptive couplings informed by noise/data distributions (e.g., via optimal transport, OT) improve both model training and inference. We radicalize this insight by shifting the paradigm: rather than computing adaptive couplings directly, we use distilled couplings from a different, pretrained model capable of placing noise and data spaces in bijection -- a property intrinsic to normalizing flows (NF) through their maximum likelihood and invertibility requirements. Leveraging recent advances in NF image generation via auto-regressive (AR) blocks, we propose Normalized Flow Matching (NFM), a new method that distills the quasi-deterministic coupling of pretrained NF models to train student flow models. These students achieve the best of both worlds: significantly outperforming flow models trained with independent or even OT couplings, while also improving on the teacher AR-NF model.

### [185] [An accurate flatness measure to estimate the generalization performance of CNN models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09016)
*Rahman Taleghani,Maryam Mohammadi,Francesco Marchetti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对卷积神经网络（CNN）提出了一种精确且架构适配的平坦度度量方法。通过推导交叉熵损失关于卷积核的Hessian迹的闭式解，并将其应用于全局平均池化后的线性分类器网络，构建了一个考虑缩放对称性和滤波器交互作用的参数化感知平坦度度量。实验结果表明该度量能有效评估CNN的泛化能力并指导架构设计。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 推导了交叉熵损失关于卷积核的Hessian迹的闭式表达式，适用于使用全局平均池化后接线性分类器的CNN架构；2. 将相对平坦度概念专门化到卷积层，构建参数化感知的平坦度度量；3. 该度量正确考虑了由卷积和池化操作引起的缩放对称性和滤波器交互作用。

Result: 在标准图像分类基准数据集上对多个CNN模型族进行了实证研究。实验结果表明，所提出的平坦度度量可以作为评估和比较CNN模型泛化性能的稳健工具，并能为实际中的架构设计和训练选择提供指导。
